**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

312026-03-11T02:42:31.045233agentmessage-
The answer has been compiled and written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary of Findings

### Frame Construction Pipeline
The CSS frame construction is implemented in **`layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp`** / `.h`. The `nsCSSFrameConstructor` class (extending `nsFrameManager`) provides `ConstructFrameFromItemInternal()`, `ConstructFramesFromItem()`, and `ConstructFramesFromItemList()` as the core frame-building functions.

### Block Layout Reflow Pipeline
The block reflow pipeline centers on **`layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.cpp`** with:
- `nsBlockFrame::Reflow()` — top-level entry point
- `nsBlockFrame::ReflowDirtyLines()` — iterates dirty lines
- `nsBlockFrame::ReflowLine()` — reflows individual lines
- `nsBlockFrame::DoReflowInlineFrames()` — drives inline reflow via `nsLineLayout`

Supporting infrastructure includes `BlockReflowState`, `nsBlockReflowContext`, `ReflowInput`, `ReflowOutput`, `nsLineLayout`, `nsLineBox`, `nsFloatManager`, `nsContainerFrame`, `AbsoluteContainingBlock`, and all the concrete frame types (`nsInlineFrame`, `nsTextFrame`, `nsFlexContainerFrame`, `nsGridContainerFrame`, etc.).

### Dirty-Frame Invalidation Mechanism
The invalidation system is driven by:
- **`layout/base/PresShell.cpp`** — `FrameNeedsReflow()` marks frames dirty and schedules reflow
- **`layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp`** — `ProcessRestyledFrames()` translates style changes into reflow requests
- **`layout/style/nsChangeHint.h`** — defines the change hint flags (`nsChangeHint_NeedReflow`, `nsChangeHint_ReconstructFrame`)
- **`layout/generic/nsLineBox.h`** — `MarkDirty()` for line-level invalidation
- **`layout/generic/nsIFrame.cpp`** — `MarkIntrinsicISizesDirty()` for intrinsic size propagation
